***brullen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:brullen.html>brullen</a> (19231)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:brullen.html>brullen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">brüelen</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">brüllen</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brullen.html>brullen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to roar</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cry (of a <a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a>)</li></ol>

***bruno.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bruno.html>bruno</a> (6106)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">brūnus</i> "brown, brunet" (whence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:bruno.html>bruno</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:brun.html>brun</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*brūn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*brūnaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">brown</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bher-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:shining.html>shining</a>, brown</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">brūn</i> "brown" (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bruin.html>bruin</a></i> "brown"), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">brūn</i> "brown" (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">braun</i> "brown"), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">brūn</i> "brown". More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">brown</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:bruno.html>bruno</a></strong> (<i>feminine singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="it">bruna</b>, <i>masculine plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="it">bruni</b>, <i>feminine plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="it">brune</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(dark) brown</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:bruno.html>bruno</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="it">bruni</b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="it">bruna</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a dark-haired person</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">brutael</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">savage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">brutal</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">savage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">brutalis</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">brūtus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crude</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***brutus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:brutus.html>brutus</a> (8435)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>An <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oscan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Oscan language">Oscan</a></span> loanword, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʷréh₂us</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βαρύς</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">barús</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">گران</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gerân</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">गुरु</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gurú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gravis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="la">brūtus</strong> (<i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">brūta</b>, <i>neuter</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">brūtum</b>); <i>first/second-declension adjective</i>
</p>
<ol><li>heavy, unwieldy</li>
<li>dull, stupid, insensible, unreasonable, irrational</li></ol>
</body>

***bub.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bub.html>bub</a> (39744)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably imitative of the sound of drinking.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bub.html>bub</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An alcoholic malt liquor, especially <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a>.
<ul><li><b>1838</b>, Samuel Morewood, <i>A Philosophical and Statistical History of the Inventions and Customs of Ancient and Modern Nations in the Manufacture and Use of Inebriating Liquors</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=txUZAAAAYAAJamp;pg=PA662amp;dq=%22bub%22%7C%22bubs%22+-intitle:%22bub%7Cbubs%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=xFcMT76qM8m0iQeOgcWYBgamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22bub%22%7C%22bubs%22%20-intitle%3A%22bub%7Cbubs%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">page 662</a>,
<dl><dd><b><a href = vnd.unilang:bub.html>Bub</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> made from ground barley and strong worts, and sometimes from strong small worts from the <a href = vnd.unilang:coolers.html>coolers</a>, properly blended and boiled with some hops, in the proportion of one pound to a barrel of worts.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bubby</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bub.html>bub</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bubs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A woman's breast.
<ul><li><b>1982</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lawrence_Durrell" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Lawrence Durrell">Lawrence Durrell</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:constance.html>Constance</a></i>, Penguin 2004 (<i>Avignon Quintet</i>), p. 631:
<dl><dd>‘<a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. Blanford, I esteem that there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> nothing more sublime in nature than a glimpse of an English lady's <b>bubs</b>.’</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Either a corruption of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">brother</i>, a modification of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a></i>, or a borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pennsylvania_German_language" class="extiw" title="w:Pennsylvania German language">Pennsylvania German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pdc"><a href = vnd.unilang:bub.html>Bub</a></i> or Southern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:bub.html>Bub</a></i> (as <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoken</a> in various communities in America before the early 20th century), ultimately thought to be derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bō-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">close [male] relation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and thus cognate to English <i>boy</i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:babe.html>babe</a></i>? (Perhaps the term <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a confluence of several of these.)
</p>
<div class="NavFrame">
<div class="NavHead" style="text-align: left;">Other probable cognates</div>
<div class="NavContent derivedterms" style="text-align: left; column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;">
<ul><li><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">bobbe</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bube</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">boy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">babbe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">little boy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:babe.html>babe</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a></i>, and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bully</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boef.html>boef</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">bôve</i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic </div></div>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bub.html>bub</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bubs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A term of familiar address; <a href = vnd.unilang:bubba.html>bubba</a>; bubby.
<ul><li><b>1857</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>. B. Aldrich, <i>What Jedd Pallfry found in the Coffin</i>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Knickerbocker" class="extiw" title="w:The Knickerbocker">The Knickerbocker</a></i>, Volume 49, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=g8gGAQAAIAAJamp;pg=PA23amp;dq=%22bub%22%7C%22bubs%22+-intitle:%22bub%7Cbubs%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=eVAMT8TRCKuOiAfZ472cBgamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22bub%22%7C%22bubs%22%20-intitle%3A%22bub%7Cbubs%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">page 23</a>,
<dl><dd>So he changed his <i>brusque</i> manner, and inquired, in a tone which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> intended to be extremely conciliatory :</dd>
<dd>‘ What′s your name, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bub.html>bub</a></b> ? ’</dd>
<dd>‘ The last one, <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> ? ’ asked <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bub.html>bub</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:looking.html>looking</a> up.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1857</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:clara.html>Clara</a> Augusta, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mrs.html>Mrs</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>Peter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dame.html>Dame</a></i>, George <a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>R</a>. Graham, <i>Graham′s Illustrated Magazine</i>, Volume 50, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=YKnPAAAAMAAJamp;pg=PA398amp;dq=%22bub%22%7C%22bubs%22+-intitle:%22bub%7Cbubs%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=n18MT8_WAYaUiAew0_D2BQamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22bub%22%7C%22bubs%22%20-intitle%3A%22bub%7Cbubs%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">page 398</a>,
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:mrs.html>Mrs</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>Peter</a> filled her pocket with the cherries — “ Victoria and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bub.html>bub</a></b> are so fond of them!” and <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> scrambled into the wagon.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A young brother; a little boy; a familiar term of address for a small boy.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bub.html>bub</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bubs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a>.</li></ol>

<p>Shortened from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bubble</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bubbly</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bub.html>bub</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bubs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Abbreviation of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bubble</i></span></span>.</li>

<ul><li><b>2003</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/50_Cent" class="extiw" title="w:50 Cent">50 Cent</a>, "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/In_da_Club" class="extiw" title="w:In da Club">In da Club</a>":
<dl><dd>"You find <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> in da club, bottle full of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bub.html>bub</a></b>"</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To throw out in <a href = vnd.unilang:bubbles.html>bubbles</a>; to bubble.

***bubba.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bubba.html>bubba</a> (12400)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly an alteration of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">brother</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bub.html>bub</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> by a young child not yet able to pronounce <i>brother</i> properly, but note similar <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> in other Germanic languages derived from Proto-Germanic <i>*bō-</i>, such as West Frisian <i>bobbe</i>, German <i>Bube</i> ("boy"), Swedish dialectal <i>babbe</i> ("little boy"), English <i><a href = vnd.unilang:babe.html>babe</a></i>, Dutch <i><a href = vnd.unilang:boef.html>boef</a></i> ("mischievous lad, <a href = vnd.unilang:rascal.html>rascal</a>"), Middle Low German <i>bōve</i>, and Icelandic <i>bófi</i>. Also compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sissy.html>sissy</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bubba.html>bubba</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bubbas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_United_States" class="extiw" title="w:Southern United States">Southern US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> childish</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Brother; <span class="use-with-mention">used as term of familiar address</span>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b>,  Caitlin <a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>R</a>. Kiernan,  <cite>Low Red Moon‎</cite>, page 27:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"<a href = vnd.unilang:hey.html>Hey</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bubba.html>bubba</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that really you? Goddamn. I <a href = vnd.unilang:haven.html>haven</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> from you in a <a href = vnd.unilang:coon.html>coon</a>'s age." / "Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:hey.html>hey</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bubba.html>bubba</a>'</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, you sonofabitch.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A working-class white male from the southern US, stereotyped as loutish.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2009</b> February 13,  Ginia Bellafante,  “A Pitcher’s Life After the Third Strike”, in  <cite>New York Times</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2009/02/13/arts/television/13east.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Will Ferrell and his creative partner, the writer and director <a href = vnd.unilang:adam.html>Adam</a> McKay, are, let’s face it, our national <a href = vnd.unilang:poets.html>poets</a> on the subject of dimwitted, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bubba.html>bubba</a></b> arrogance and the redemptive powers of failure, their poems seemingly conceived in a midnight frenzy of brilliance on the back of a bag of Doritos.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>2011</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Steven_Pinker" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Steven Pinker"><a href = vnd.unilang:steven.html>Steven</a> Pinker</a>, <i>The Better Angels of Our Nature</i>, Penguin 2012, page 120:
<dl><dd>Their <a href = vnd.unilang:subjects.html>subjects</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> not <b>bubbas</b> from the bayous but affluent students at the University of Michigan who <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> lived in the South for at least six years.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<p>Originally a variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bobbel</i>. ***buccaneer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buccaneer.html>buccaneer</a> (76835)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">boucanier</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">boucaner</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to smoke or broil meat and fish, to hunt wild beasts for their <a href = vnd.unilang:skins.html>skins</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">boucan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grill (Native American Style)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tupi_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tupi language">Old Tupi</a></span></span> <i>mokaém</i> "grill"
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:buccaneer.html>buccaneer</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">buccaneers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of a group of seamen who cruised on their own account on the Spanish Main and in the Pacific in the 17th century; similar to <a href = vnd.unilang:pirates.html>pirates</a> but <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> not prey on ships of their own nation.</li>
<li>A pirate.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">privateer</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">pirate</span>, see also Thesaurus:pirate</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:buccaneer.html>buccaneer</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">buccaneers</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">buccaneering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">buccaneered</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To engage in piracy against any but one's own nation's ships.
<ul><li><b>1963</b>, John Day, Arthur <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bullen.html>Bullen</a> (editor), <i>The Works of John Day</i>, page v
<dl><dd>In 1596 and 1597 he <b>bucaneered</b> against Sao Thomi, the Portuguese slaving settlement off the coast of West Africa, and in the Spanish Main</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bucolisch.html>bucolisch</a> (132751)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">būcolicus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βουκολικός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boukolikós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***bud.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a> (5148)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Comparison_between_bud_and_cigarette_pack.jpg/170px-Comparison_between_bud_and_cigarette_pack.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="227" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Comparison_between_bud_and_cigarette_pack.jpg/255px-Comparison_between_bud_and_cigarette_pack.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Comparison_between_bud_and_cigarette_pack.jpg/340px-Comparison_between_bud_and_cigarette_pack.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1536" data-file-height="2048" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A marijuana <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a></b></div></div></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">budde</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a>, seed pod</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*buddǭ</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bot.html>bot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hagebutte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hip, rosehip</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, regional <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Butzen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seed pod</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Swedish dialect <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">bodd</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰew-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bu-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to swell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:buds.html>buds</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A newly sprouted leaf or blossom that <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> not yet unfolded.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">budset</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">After a long, cold winter, the trees finally began to produce <b><a href = vnd.unilang:buds.html>buds</a></b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Something that <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begun.html>begun</a> to develop.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">breast <b><a href = vnd.unilang:buds.html>buds</a></b></i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A small rounded body in the process of splitting from an organism, which may grow into a genetically identical new organism.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">In this slide, you can see a yeast cell forming <b><a href = vnd.unilang:buds.html>buds</a></b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Potent cannabis <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> from the flowering part of the plant (the “bud”), or marijuana generally.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">nug</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">marijuana</span>; <i>see also</i> Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">marijuana</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hey.html>Hey</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bro.html>bro</a>, want to smoke some <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a></b>?</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A weaned calf in its first year, so called because the horns are then beginning to <a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> term of <a href = vnd.unilang:endearment.html>endearment</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A pretty young girl.
<ul><li><b>1874</b>, <i>Lippincott's Monthly Magazine, a Popular Journal of General Literature</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">My pretty <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> unfolding and I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> not there to see it. She <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> developing so rapidly, I felt I could not be from her a day without missing some sweetness that could never come again.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:buds.html>buds</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">budding</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">budded</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To form <a href = vnd.unilang:buds.html>buds</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The trees are finally starting to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a></b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To reproduce by splitting off <a href = vnd.unilang:buds.html>buds</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Yeast reproduces by <b>budding</b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To begin to grow, or to issue from a stock in the manner of a <a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a>, as a horn.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To be like a <a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a> in respect to youth and freshness, or growth and promise.
<ul><li><b>1594</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Taming_of_the_Shrew" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Taming of the Shrew">The Taming of the Shrew</a></i>
<dl><dd>Young <b>budding</b> virgin, fair and fresh and sweet, / Whither away, or where <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> thy abode?</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To put forth as a <a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a>.
<ul><li><b>2013</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:julie.html>Julie</a> Brown, <i>The Brownstone</i> (page 263)
<dl><dd>What appeared the same to us really wasn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a>. Every day <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> different, if <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> looked closely enough. Like the topiary tree that finally <b>budded</b> a <a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a> after Terrence died: <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To graft by inserting a <a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a> under the bark of another tree.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Back-formation from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:buddy.html>buddy</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:buds.html>buds</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Canada, US</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:buddy.html>Buddy</a>, friend.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <i>see</i> Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">friend</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">I like to hang out with my <b><a href = vnd.unilang:buds.html>buds</a></b> on Saturday night.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2018</b> November 27,  April Wolfe,  “<i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anna_and_the_Apocalypse" class="extiw" title="w:Anna and the Apocalypse"><a href = vnd.unilang:anna.html>Anna</a> And The Apocalypse</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a Holiday-horror Cocktail of <a href = vnd.unilang:singing.html>Singing</a>, Maiming, and Clichés”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_A.V._Club" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The A.V. Club">The A.V. Club</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20191104041033/https://www.avclub.com/anna-and-the-apocalypse-is-a-holiday-horror-cocktail-of-1830660900">[1]</a></sup>, archived from <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.avclub.com/anna-and-the-apocalypse-is-a-holiday-horror-cocktail-of-1830660900">the original</a> on <span class="mw-formatted-date" title="2019-11-04">4 November 2019</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:anna.html>Anna</a>'s <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a></b>, John (Malcolm Cumming), harbors a secret crush on her, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> indicative of the lazier, more derivative portions of the story that simply repeat tropes rather than comment on them.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buddies.html>buddies</a> (44008)</h1><br></body> 
***buddy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buddy.html>buddy</a> (3833)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1802, colloquial <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">butty</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">companion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, also the form of an older dialect term meaning workmate, associated with coal mining. Itself believed derived from 1530 as <i>booty fellow</i>, a partner with whom one shares booty or loot.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Alternatively, an alteration of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">brother</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:buddy.html>buddy</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:buddies.html>buddies</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A friend or casual acquaintance.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mate.html>mate</a></span>; <i>see also</i> Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">friend</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">They have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:buddies.html>buddies</a></b> since they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> in school.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A partner for a particular activity.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">companion</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">partner</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">drinking <b><a href = vnd.unilang:buddies.html>buddies</a></b></i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>An informal and friendly address to a stranger; a friendly placeholder name for a person one does not know.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mate.html>mate</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">fellow</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hey.html>Hey</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:buddy.html>buddy</a></b>, I think you dropped this.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:buddy.html>buddy</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:buddies.html>buddies</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">buddying</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">buddied</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To assign a <a href = vnd.unilang:buddy.html>buddy</a>, or partner, to.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b>,  Philip Briggs amp; Danny Edmunds,  <cite>Mozambique: The Bradt Travel Guide</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=cJ8ZJaxdbIQC">[1]</a></sup>, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 86:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">If you are being formally <b>buddied</b>, have a good chat with your <a href = vnd.unilang:buddy.html>buddy</a> and find out their interests <a href = vnd.unilang:--.html>--</a> these should more or less match your own.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:buddy.html>buddy</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:buddy.html>buddy</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:buddy.html>buddy</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Resembling a <a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a>.
<ul><li><b>1963</b>, John Herbert Goddard, <i>Chrysanthemum Growers' Treasury</i> (page 18)
<dl><dd>Some of the dwarfer varieties are full of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:buddy.html>buddy</a></b> growths in the early <a href = vnd.unilang:stages.html>stages</a> and these must be cut down and thrown away.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***budge.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a> (52265)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">bougier</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">bougier</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*bullicāre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bubble; seethe; move; stir</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bullīre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to boil; seethe; roil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">budges</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">budging</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">budged</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To move.
<dl><dd><i>I’ve <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> pushing this rock as hard as I can, but it <a href = vnd.unilang:won.html>won</a>’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a></b> an inch.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1590–1592</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Taming_of_the_Shrew" class="extiw" title="w:The Taming of the Shrew">The Taming of the Shrew</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act PROLOGUE, scene i]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> not <b><a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a></b> an inch, boy.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>2014</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:jacob.html>Jacob</a> Steinberg, "<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.theguardian.com/football/2014/mar/09/manchester-city-wigan-athletic-fa-cup">Wigan shock Manchester City in FA Cup again to reach semi-finals</a>", <i>The Guardian</i>, 9 March 2014:
<dl><dd>Yet <a href = vnd.unilang:goals.html>goals</a> in either <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> from Jordi Gómez and James Perch inspired them and then, in the face of a relentless City onslaught, they simply would not <b><a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a></b>, throwing heart, body and soul in the way of a ball which seemed destined for their <a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a> on several <a href = vnd.unilang:occasions.html>occasions</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To move.
<dl><dd><i>I’ve <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> pushing this rock as hard as I can, but I can’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a></b> it.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>To yield in one’s opinions or beliefs.
<dl><dd><i>The Minister for Finance refused to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a></b> on the new economic rules.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Minnesota<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Wisconsin<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Iowa<span class="ib-comma">,</span> western  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canada" class="extiw" title="w:Canada">Canada</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cut or butt (in line); to join the front or middle rather than the back of a queue.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hey.html>Hey</a>, no <b>budging</b>! Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a></b> in line!</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>To try to improve the spot of a decision on a sports field.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> add an example for this sense?)</span></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">shift</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>In senses 1-3, most often used in negative senses (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:won.html>won</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a>; refused to <a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a></i>, but not usually <i>Sure, I'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a></i> or <i>Will he <a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a>?</i>); but see <i><a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a> up</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Brisk; stirring; jocund.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of South to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">bouge</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bulga</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a leathern bag or knapsack</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bulge</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of fur prepared from lambskin dressed with the wool on, formerly used as an edging and ornament, especially on scholastic habits.
<ul><li><b>1649</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Milton" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Milton">John Milton</a>, <i>Observations</i>
<dl><dd>They are become so liberal, as to part freely with their own <b><a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a></b>-gowns from off their <a href = vnd.unilang:backs.html>backs</a>.}}</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">budge</strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>

***buffel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buffel.html>buffel</a> (21992)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:buffel.html>buffel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">buffle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">bufalo</i> (archaic <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">buffalo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bubalus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βούβαλος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boúbalos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buffel.html>buffel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buffels.html>buffels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buffel.html>buffeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A buffalo, one of some mammals of the subfamily Bovinae, especially of the genus <i>Bubalus</i> or <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Syncerus_caffer" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Syncerus caffer"><i>Syncerus caffer</i></a></span>.</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:zoogdieren.html>zoogdieren</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> verzamelnaam <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aantal.html>aantal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zware.html>zware</a> holhoornige rundersoorten <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:forse.html>forse</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoorns.html>hoorns</a>

***bugle.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a> (61527)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">buculus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">young bull; ox; steer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/A_bugler_from_the_Band_of_HM_Royal_Marines_Portsmouth_%28Royal_Band%29_sounding_a_bugle_call..jpg/220px-A_bugler_from_the_Band_of_HM_Royal_Marines_Portsmouth_%28Royal_Band%29_sounding_a_bugle_call..jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/A_bugler_from_the_Band_of_HM_Royal_Marines_Portsmouth_%28Royal_Band%29_sounding_a_bugle_call..jpg/330px-A_bugler_from_the_Band_of_HM_Royal_Marines_Portsmouth_%28Royal_Band%29_sounding_a_bugle_call..jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/A_bugler_from_the_Band_of_HM_Royal_Marines_Portsmouth_%28Royal_Band%29_sounding_a_bugle_call..jpg/440px-A_bugler_from_the_Band_of_HM_Royal_Marines_Portsmouth_%28Royal_Band%29_sounding_a_bugle_call..jpg 2x" data-file-width="4928" data-file-height="3280" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A soldier playing a <a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a>.</div></div></div>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bugles</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A horn used by hunters.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a simple brass instrument consisting of a horn with no valves, playing only pitches in its harmonic series</li>
<li>A plant in the family Lamiaceae grown as a ground cover, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Ajuga_reptans" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Ajuga reptans"><i>Ajuga reptans</i></a></span>, and other plants in the genus <i>Ajuga</i>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">bugleweed</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">carpet <a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">ground pine</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>Anything shaped like a <a class="mw-selflink selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a></a>, round or conical and having a bell on one end.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">shaped like a <a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">cone</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">funnel</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">bugles</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">bugling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">bugled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To announce, sing, or cry in the manner of a musical <a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">trumpet</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bugulus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a woman's ornament</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bugles</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a tubular glass or plastic bead sewn onto <a href = vnd.unilang:clothes.html>clothes</a> as a decorative trim
<ul><li><b>1925</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/P._G._Wodehouse" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:P. G. Wodehouse">P. G. Wodehouse</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sam_the_Sudden" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Sam the Sudden"><a href = vnd.unilang:sam.html>Sam</a> the Sudden</a></i>, Random House, London:2007, p. 207.
<dl><dd>With the exception of a woman in a black silk dress with <b>bugles</b> who, incredible as it may seem, <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> ordered cocoa and sparkling limado simultaneously and <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> washing down a meal of Cambridge sausages and pastry with alternate draughts of both liquids, the place <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> empty.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> jet-black
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1598–1600</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/As_You_Like_It" class="extiw" title="w:As You Like It">As You Like It</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buidel.html>buidel</a> (28849)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">budel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">būdil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*buzdô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beetle, <a href = vnd.unilang:grub.html>grub</a>, swelling</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰūs-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move quickly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Beutel</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buigen.html>buigen</a> (5036)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bugen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*būgan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*būganą</i>, a variant form of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*beuganą</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">buse</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. ***buit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buit.html>buit</a> (4607)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>16th century, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">büte</i>, whence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Beute</i> and eventually all other related forms.  Of uncertain ultimate origin; possibly a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Celtic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Celtic languages">Celtic</a></span> borrowing, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*boudi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">victory, booty, spoils</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 1 | </a></sup>  If so, related to the name of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Boudica" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Boudica">Boudica</a>, a British Celtic queen.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 2 | </a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>

***buitensluiten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buitensluiten.html>buitensluiten</a> (25003)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buiten.html>buiten</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sluiten.html>sluiten</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buitensluiten.html>buitensluiten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shut out, to lock out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to exclude, to shun</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
